\DoxyCodeLine{00575\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ of\ up\ to\ 23\ chars\ on\ the\ stack\ before\ going\ on\ the\ heap\ -\/\ the\ last\ byte\ of\ the\ buffer\ is\ used\ for:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00576\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ "{}is\ small"{}\ bit\ -\/\ the\ highest\ bit\ -\/\ if\ "{}0"{}\ then\ it\ is\ small\ -\/\ otherwise\ its\ "{}1"{}\ (128)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00577\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ if\ small\ -\/\ capacity\ left\ before\ going\ on\ the\ heap\ -\/\ using\ the\ lowest\ 5\ bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00578\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ if\ small\ -\/\ 2\ bits\ are\ left\ unused\ -\/\ the\ second\ and\ third\ highest\ ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00579\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ if\ small\ -\/\ acts\ as\ a\ null\ terminator\ if\ strlen()\ is\ 23\ (24\ including\ the\ null\ terminator)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00580\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ the\ "{}is\ small"{}\ bit\ remains\ "{}0"{}\ ("{}as\ well\ as\ the\ capacity\ left"{})\ so\ its\ OK}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03605\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Provides\ a\ multilane\ implementation\ of\ an\ atomic\ variable\ that\ supports\ add,\ sub,\ load,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03606\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ store.\ Instead\ of\ using\ a\ single\ atomic\ variable,\ this\ splits\ up\ into\ multiple\ ones,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03607\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ each\ sitting\ on\ a\ separate\ cache\ line.\ The\ goal\ is\ to\ provide\ a\ speedup\ when\ most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03608\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ operations\ are\ modifying.\ It\ achieves\ this\ with\ two\ properties:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03609\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03610\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ *\ Multiple\ atomics\ are\ used,\ so\ chance\ of\ congestion\ from\ the\ same\ atomic\ is\ reduced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03611\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ *\ Each\ atomic\ sits\ on\ a\ separate\ cache\ line,\ so\ false\ sharing\ is\ reduced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03612\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03613\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ disadvantage\ is\ that\ there\ is\ a\ small\ overhead\ due\ to\ the\ use\ of\ TLS,\ and\ load/store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03614\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ is\ slower\ because\ all\ atomics\ have\ to\ be\ accessed.}}
